The app is perfect for a quick reference guide to help identify a bird by sound or sighting, or anyone who is looking to improve their knowledge of British birds.\r\n\r\nPlease Note: Tweeter Bird Sounds must not be used as a means to attract birds! It's intended purely as a learning resource. Attracting wild birds using recorded sounds disturbs and confuses them, disrupting their natural behaviours (such as foraging). Thank you for using the app responsibly.\r\n\r\nFeatures:\r\n- Over 200 species and over 500 sounds\r\n- A-Z jump list to find specific species easily\r\n- Birds also grouped by families e.g. finches\r\n- Create a favourites list for quick access to particular birds\r\n- Create a checklist of birds you’ve seen/heard\r\n- Profile for each species containing soundboard, photo, RSPB description and links to extended recordings and original photos\r\n- Sounds divided into songs, calls, alarms etc.\r\n- Links to each birds RSPB profile\r\n- It’s FREE and free of adverts!\r\n\r\nWe hope Tweeter will be a useful learning tool for you.
